<script type="text/javascript">
  $(window).load(function() {
    var now = new Date();
    if ( getCookie("bylzobrazensplash") != now.getDate() )
    {
      $('#splashscreen').modal();
      setInterval( function(){zavri_splashscreen()},12500 );
      setCookie("bylzobrazensplash",now.getDate(),31)
    } 
  });
  //alert( getCookie("bylzobrazensplash") );
  function zavri_splashscreen() { $.modal.close(); }
  function getCookie(c_name)
  {
  var i,x,y,ARRcookies=document.cookie.split(";");
  for (i=0;i<ARRcookies.length;i++)
  {
    x=ARRcookies[i].substr(0,ARRcookies[i].indexOf("="));
    y=ARRcookies[i].substr(ARRcookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);
    x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");
    if (x==c_name)
      {
      return unescape(y);
      }
    }
  }
  function setCookie(c_name,value,exdays)
  {
  var exdate=new Date();
  exdate.setDate(exdate.getDate() + exdays);
  var c_value=escape(value) + ((exdays==null) ? "" : "; expires="+exdate.toUTCString());
  document.cookie=c_name + "=" + c_value;
  }
</script>

  function addMarker(location, xtitle, ico, id, bublina, show) 
  {
    show = show || 0;
    var iconimage = new google.maps.MarkerImage( 'http://www.ceskybenzin.cz/gmapa/mm_20_'+ico+'.png', null, null, null, new google.maps.Size(12,20) );
    var image = 'http://www.ceskybenzin.cz/gmapa/mm_20_'+ico+'.png';
    pole_marker[id] = new google.maps.Marker({
      position: location,
      map: map,
      icon: iconimage,
      title: xtitle
    });
    pole_bublin[id] = new google.maps.InfoWindow({ content: bublina });
    google.maps.event.addListener(pole_marker[id], 'click', function() 
    {
      if ( infowindowlast ) { pole_bublin[infowindowlast].close();  }
      infowindowlast = id;
      pole_bublin[id].open( map,pole_marker[id] ); 
    });
    if ( show == 1 ) { infowindowlast = id; pole_bublin[id].open( map,pole_marker[id] ); }
  }
  
  function geocode(opts) {
    function geocodeResult(response, status) {
      if (status == google.maps.GeocoderStatus.OK && response[0]) {
        document.getElementById("search").value = response[0].formatted_address;
        map.fitBounds(response[0].geometry.viewport);
      } else {
        alert("Sorry, " + status);
      }
    } // trim leading and trailing space with capable browsers
    if(opts.address && opts.address.trim)opts.address = opts.address.trim(); 
    if(opts.address || opts.latLng)geocoder.geocode(opts, geocodeResult); // no empty request
  }  
  google.maps.event.addListener(map, 'idle', function() {
    infowindowlast = 0;
    pole_bublin[0].open( map,pole_marker[0] ); 
  });
  
  </script>

  &nbsp;&nbsp;<input type="text" size="20" name="search" id="search" onchange="geocode({address:this.value})" onclick="$('#search').val('')">
  &nbsp;&nbsp;<input type="button" id="address_subm" class="inpsubm" value="Vyhledat" onclick="geocode({ address:$('#search').val() })">

    <script type="text/javascript">
        
      function test() 
      {  
        var emailReg = /^([\w-\.]+@([\w-]+\.)+[\w-]{2,4})?$/; 
        if ( $("#form2 #inputtext1a").val() == "OK" && $("#form2 #inputtext3").val() == $("#form2 #inputtext2").val() && $("#form2 #inputtext3").val().length > 3 && $("#form2 #inputtext1").val().length > 3 && emailReg.test( $("#form2 #inputtext11").val() ) ) 
        { return true; } else { return false; }
      }
      
      function testjmeno()
      {
          $.ajax({
            url: "/ajax_test_user.php",
            type: "POST",
            cache: false,
            data: { jmeno : $("#form2 #inputtext1").val() },
            dataType: "html",
            success: function(html){
              if ( html.length > 3 ) { $("#form2 #inputtext1").css("background-color", "#98fb98"); $("#form2 #inputtext1a").val("OK"); }
              else { $("#form2 #inputtext1").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); $("#form2 #inputtext1a").val("KO"); }   
            }
          });
      } 

      function zobraz_reg_okno()
      {
        $("#login").hide();
        $("#newlogin").show();
        // username
        $("#form2 #inputtext1").keyup(function () {
          if ( $("#form2 #inputtext1").val().length < 4 ) { $("#form2 #inputtext1").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); } 
          else { testjmeno(); }
        }); 
        // heslo1
        $("#form2 #inputtext2").keyup(function () {
          if ( $("#form2 #inputtext2").val().length < 4 ) { $("#form2 #inputtext3,#form2 #inputtext2").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); } 
          else {  if ( $("#form2 #inputtext2").val() == $("#form2 #inputtext3").val() ) { $("#form2 #inputtext3,#form2 #inputtext2").css("background-color", "#98fb98"); } else { { $("#form2 #inputtext3,#form2 inputtext2").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); } }  }
        });
        //heslo2 
        $("#form2 #inputtext3").keyup(function () {
          if ( $("#form2 #inputtext3").val().length < 4 ) { $("#form2 #inputtext3,#form2 #inputtext2").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); } 
          else {  if ( $("#form2 #inputtext3").val() == $("#form2 #inputtext2").val() ) { $("#form2 #inputtext3,#form2 #inputtext2").css("background-color", "#98fb98"); } else { { $("#form2 #inputtext3,#form2 #inputtext2").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); } }  }
        }); 
        // email
        $("#form2 #inputtext11").keyup(function () {
          var emailReg = /^([\w-\.]+@([\w-]+\.)+[\w-]{2,4})?$/;
          if ( !emailReg.test( $("#form2 #inputtext11").val() ) ) { $("#form2 #inputtext11").css("background-color", "#ff6347"); } 
          else { $("#form2 #inputtext11").css("background-color", "#98fb98"); }
        });
        $("#form2 #inputtext1").focus();
        return false;
      }    

    $(document).ready(function() {
      $("#form1").validate({
        rules: {
          inputtext1: { required: true },
          inputtext2: { required: true }
        },
        messages:{
          inputtext2: '', inputtext1: ''
        }                  
      });
    });
    
    </script> 

    <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function() { 
      $.ajax({
        url: "/ajax_stat_user.php",
        cache: false,
        success: function(html){
          if ( html.length > 3 ) { $("#login").replaceWith(html); }
        }
      });
    }); 
    </script>
